       <h2 class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title trb_outfit_featuredArticleTitle">
        <a class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title_a" href="/health/ct-why-we-re-so-scared-of-gmos-20150706-story.html#navtype=outfit">
         Why we're so scared of GMOs, according to someone who has studied them since the start
        </a>
        <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets">
         <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets_1">
         </span>
        </span>
       </h2>
       <div class="trb_bylines">
        <span class="trb_bylines_name_primary">
         <span class="trb_bylines_name_author" data-byline-withoutby="">
          <span itemprop="author">
           Roberto A. Ferdman
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </div>
       <p class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_content">
        <span class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_content_text">
         When Chipotle announced that it would no longer serve food made with GMOs due to safety concerns, customers rejoiced. But there was one big problem: Just as more Americans grow wary of GMOs, the scientific community is moving in the opposite direction.
        </span>
       </p>
      </article>
     </section>

         <h3 class="trb_outfit_relatedListTitle">
          <a class="trb_outfit_relatedListTitle_a" href="/local/palm-beach/fl-terminally-ill-drugs-20150619-story.html#navtype=outfit">
           Terminally ill in Florida win better access to experimental drugs
          </a>
          <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets">
           <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets_1">
           </span>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p class="trb_outfit_group_list_item_brief">
          As an activist for people with grave illnesses, Deb Gaudet strongly supported passage of a new Florida law called the Right to Try Act, which takes effect July 1 and attempts to make it easier for terminally ill people to obtain treatments not yet approved by the FDA.
         </p>
